< Text>
Decent job on my dip powder nails but way overpriced. A $25 pedicure should involve more than removing my old polish and putting another color on. No scrub, lotion, or anything. Their removal process for the dip powder was to soak my finger tips in a bowl of acetone for over half an hour. For $50, you‚Äôd think maybe a hand massage or cuticle cut down: nope. Just removing the dip powder and putting it back on after reshaping. Disappointing. I will try another place next time.

Edit: have returned and gotten MUCH better service. It is a hit or a miss, just had to find the manicurists that I felt like met my needs. Eyelash extensions for a good price, too.< /Text>

<review>I can cook canned food at home. Disappointed, and will not return.
My wife and I came to this restaurant to get a Saturday morning breakfast. This sounded like just the right kind of place for a satisfying meal. I was craving hash browns in particular.
The first disappointment was the coffee. It barely tasted like anything. I've had lots of diner coffee but this was among the worst.
I was really excited to find corned beef hash on the menu. I love it, love making it, and I expected that a "home-cooked" place like this might actually make their own. Nope, they upended a can of cheap corned beef hash on the griddle, flipped it over, and put the greasy mass on my plate. Second, my side of hash browns was really hard on the outside, yet dry and soft on the inside. How do you ruin hash browns?
We had more problems, as my wife's plate was unpalatable. Eggs scrambled with chips and chorizo is NOT chilaquiles. Thankfully, they did not make us pay for her plate or coffee, and we went to the Mexican grocery store down the road to get some decent food for her.
I'm giving Grammas Country Kitchen 2 stars instead of 1 because they tried to fix the problem with my wife's food and were polite about it, but we left very dissatisfied and will not return. Next time I want to eat canned corned beef hash ill buy a can of Libby's (not whatever can they bought) and cook it at home, where I can also get decent coffee.<//review><Resp>None<//Resp></record></dataset><record>

<review>At a Glance:
Food: 3.5 - 4.5
Service: 4
Convenience: 3-4
Value: 3.5 - 4
Bottom Line: This is a 4-4.5 star place in my book. Which is, on my scale, as good as it gets. A great spot for a home-style cafe/diner-type meal and experience that the chain restaurants in the area can't seem to match. With so many options this might be a place you can just come to and be confident you'll be happy.
.
.
The Boring Details:
Food:
Lots of the standard cafe/diner options are available. They seemed to have a lot of pie choices. We didn't have any this time. Had I not been so full I would have gobbled up a slice or two and wash it down with one of the big cinnamon rolls.
Everything we ate was good. The surprise for me were the potatoes. Great mix of flavors and a nice crust on the outside of the pillowy soft insides.  If it had a little more "crust" on it I think I could have just ate them by themselves.
Pancakes were big and filling. I initially thought that I wouldn't like them because they were so thick. I prefer them a little thinner. But they were good.
The only thing I thought was OK were the Biscuits. The texture was a little more crumbly then I like. So more of a preference then a true detractor since I'd eat them again.

Service: 4
The people we dealt with with were friendly and efficient.
Food came out in a reasonable amount of time.

Convenience: 3-4
Parking is ample and the location was easy to find. I also like that there is parking for RVs and larger vehicles. I hate finding food on the road. So having an option like this (other than a truck stop) when I'm pulling a trailer is pretty neat.

Value: 3.5 - 4
Dining out is getting expensive. There were a lot of great specials. So for the overall experience I think I found our new breakfast spot along the 10 corridor.<//review><Pics>None<//Pics><Response>None</Response>< gmap_id>

< Review>
I'm shocked by the positive reviews. Angie was our server and was outstanding. The food was dreadful. They promote "homemade" but use "" because clearly most of the food is not.

We had tater tot appetizer and those were fairly good. My wife had the monte cristo and the turkey tasted rancid. I had the Salisbury steak and mashed potatoes. It was luke warm and had no flavor at all.  I figured the biscuits had to be good right? Wrong. Dry and flavorless even the jam they served with it had no flavor.

The place is old but clean. Needs new flooring.

We read the reviews and were excited to try it because we love comfort food. We were very disappointed.  They need to cut the menu down by 50% and focus on making authentic fresh made comfort food with some flavor.

We are not harsh food critics. We like simple fresh food. Our experience is quite different than what most of these reviews say. The staff however is exceptional.<//Review>

<Resp>None< /Resp>< Text>
Dashed into Banning for some fuel and saw this unique, inviting local fav with a parking lot full of cars.  Walked inside to an adorable,  family friendly,  definitely like grandma's house kinda place.  The staff was great,  very attentive.   If this review was only about the staff and building it would be 5 full stars,  but, lets get real..we stopped for food.  There was 4 of us.  Dinner and dessert...over $100.00.
We ordered two Ribeye's, one chicken sandwich,  drinks and dessert.   The drinks are large and generous,  great value.   The steaks were not like the drinks...left 3/4 of them on the plate due to fat.   The chicken sandwich's bread was too soggy to eat..so, you guessed it.  Left it on the plate.  The pies...hhhmmm, we were a bit puzzled.  Was it Coconut or Banana??  None of us tasted coconut....All we tasted was instant pudding...in banana flavor.  Sorry Gramma but my next trip to Cali will not include a visit....  :  (< /Text>
